Important News

Central and National Government Memorial Week 50

▲ The Central Party Headquarters held its 68th Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week at 9:00 AM on July 14th in the auditorium. Attendees included Central Committee members Chen Guofu, Liu Lu Yin, Chen Lifu, Yu Jingtang, and staff from various departments and invited guests, totaling approximately 500 people. Chairman Chen Guofu presided. After the ceremony, Yu Jingtang delivered a report, briefly stating that regarding recent military developments, Zhang Guijun's forces intruding into Hunan province have been severely defeated by the Central Army and are nearing complete annihilation. As for the enemy on the Longhai Railway, Shi Yousan's troops have largely surrendered their weapons and are no longer capable of fighting. The Jin Army under Zhang Huizhao on the Jinpu Railway

Page 8

have been routed by the Central Army and dare not attempt to invade southward again. Jinan can be recovered soon. Viewing the overall military situation, it is certain that the rebels can be eliminated in short order and that final victory will be achieved. Regarding the two factions of the Western Hills Group, although they have been active in the north for a long time, they are actually at odds with each other, each pursuing their own agendas and competing for power. The so-called cadre meeting initiated earlier this month was much ado about nothing. In the end, the two factions' opinions clashed like fire and water, making unity impossible, and the matter was dropped. Recently, due to the Central Army's repeated victories, they attempted to cover up information from the northerners and prevent panic in the rear by holding a so-called enlarged meeting. This was purely a pointless act of self-deception. The result was further discord between the military, government, and party. Chen Gongbo did send a telegram to Wang Jingwei, stating that the northern finances were unsustainable, party affairs were increasingly chaotic, he could not continue, and was prepared to leave. Wang also replied by telegram to Chen, saying that discussing the party with them was impossible, that he would not come north, and that Chen should not leave hastily to avoid being ridiculed. The situation in the north can be seen from this. At a time when the reactionary forces have not yet been eliminated, how to advance politics and improve party affairs is truly the work and responsibility that our comrades must absolutely bear. Since the reorganization of party affairs in the 17th year of the Republic, there has been considerable progress, but imperfections are unavoidable, which we must acknowledge. Although the criticisms from inside and outside the party regarding the party's achievements and the attacks on those responsible are often superficial and lack grounding in reality, we should reflect on ourselves and be more vigilant. Lower-level party branches have several shortcomings: (1) too much emphasis on appearances, often with thoughts of overstepping their bounds, neglecting their actual work and showing little results; (2) merely conduits for orders from higher-level party branches, lacking vitality; (3) ignorance of the meaning of division of labor and cooperation, with those responsible for propaganda considering the organization and training departments as completely separate; (4) when disagreeing with the instructions of higher-level party branches, not presenting reasons and applying for reconsideration based on party discipline, but instead distributing flyers and engaging in attacks. All these points must be corrected. In the future, the entire party should strive for innovation. In all work, remain still when stillness is appropriate, without resorting to oversimplification; act when action is appropriate, without acting rashly; have a positive spirit and strive for the progress of the party and the development of all undertakings, so that the national revolution can be completed as soon as possible. This is what I have to offer to you all today, etc. The meeting adjourned at 10:00 AM after the report.

The National Government held Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week at 10:00 AM on the same morning. Attendees included Gu Yingfen, Zhu Peide, Ma Fuxiang, Jiang Menglin, Liu Ruiheng, Zhang Nanxian, Chen Yi, Chen Shaokuan, Lin Xiang, Zhang Wohua, Chen Yu, Ju Siyu, and over 200 staff from the two departments of civil officials and military advisors of the National Government. Chairman Gu Yingfen presided. After the ceremony, Secretary Qian Changzhao delivered a report. (Three months ago) I raised the issue of self-determination for Far Eastern nations. At that time, Indian nonviolent resistance had just begun, the revolutionary forces in Annam were growing, and the Philippine Independence Congress issued a declaration listing reasons for demanding autonomy. The atmosphere surrounding the Korean independence movement was tense. In the past three months, no significant developments have been heard from Korea. In the Philippines, the declaration of independence by the Independence Congress has not been approved by the United States, causing great resentment among the general population and a tendency to continue until the goal is achieved, with specific expressions such as student strikes. However, judging from the current attitude of the United States towards the Philippines, Philippine independence will probably not be achieved immediately. The revolution in Annam is intensifying daily, with many young people sacrificing themselves as a result. French high-pressure tactics may not be able to solve the problem completely. The influence of nonviolent resistance in India is very significant and is worth studying in detail. Four points should be noted in nonviolent resistance: (1) the general awakening of the Indian people. Although religions, languages, and classes differ throughout India, all areas have followed suit since the beginning of this nonviolent resistance. The number of those arrested has reached three to four thousand, and their courage has not diminished. (2) the appeal of Gandhi's personality and the efforts of his followers. Gandhi has fought for 40 years and has been imprisoned several times. This fearless spirit is not only revered in India but also influences foreigners who happen to meet him. After reading Dr. Aet's speech, one can imagine the attractiveness of Gandhi's personality. Reading the conversation between Gandhi and the Commissioner Shorokomb in prison is even more admirable. Some say that the Indian nationalist movement is centered on Gandhi, which is no exaggeration. As for Gandhi's followers, such as Taiboji, they all have unwavering determination and have always fought in accordance with Gandhi's principles. When Gandhi was arrested and a meeting of 100,000 people became very emotional, he calmly announced the absolute avoidance of violence. His ability to implement the principles of nonviolent resistance is truly unmatched. Now that Taiboji and others have also been arrested, there are many who follow. (3) the political power of the All-India National Congress. Since the beginning of non-violent resistance, the National Congress has fought in unison with Gandhi, and its leaders, such as Nehru, have been very diligent. Now that Nehru and others have been arrested, the work of the National Congress headquarters and the National Congresses in various provinces is still ongoing. (4) the participation of Indian women in nonviolent resistance is also very important. Mrs. Naidu, Mrs. Munshi, and Mrs. Kaipteng have all been arrested for this reason, but many women continue their efforts and are not intimidated, which is commendable. As mentioned above, the impact of nonviolent resistance is so great that Britain is finding it difficult to cope. Recently, those in Britain who sympathize with India include the Independent Labour Party, which has expressed itself at times, and women's groups have held meetings to resolve to petition the government, and Canon Belden of the Central Church in London occasionally made statements on humanitarian grounds, but nothing else has been heard. There are also very few who advocate using force to solve the Indian problem. The majority hope to solve everything with the planned Round Table Conference, but even if the Round Table Conference is convened, the outcome is difficult to predict. If Britain uses the Simon Commission report as the basis for discussion, India may not be satisfied, and Britain may not fully accept the various conditions put forward by India. The future is not optimistic. Let's see how things change in the future. Domestically, in terms of military affairs, the insurgent side on the Jinpu Railway is receiving support in their difficulties, but they will certainly collapse soon. The rebel forces on the Longhai and Pinghan Railways have suffered almost complete losses and can be eliminated soon. Zhang Guijun's remaining rebels have been completely defeated by us and should not be a problem in the future. The communist bandits in Jiangxi are taking advantage of the situation to attempt to succeed, but they have also been successively suppressed. The overall situation is very optimistic. Recently, the weather has been unusually hot, and the frontline generals and soldiers are working very hard. We in the rear should make twice the effort.

Contact Between Korean and Jin Armies on the Jiaoji Railway 51

Qingdao-Jinan traffic completely interrupted.

Four-nation consuls discuss maintaining traffic.

Jinan dispatch: After the Korean army retreated from the east, it actively deployed on the Jiaoji Line, planning a counterattack. On the evening of the 5th, the Korean and Jin armies began to make contact. On the Jin army side on the Jiaoji Line, the front was the 5th Army of Li Fuying, the left wing was the 3rd Army of Wang Jingguo, and the right wing was the 9th Army of Feng Pengzhu. There was also the newly formed 1st Army concurrently commanded by the 1st Division Commander Shi Fengming, who was responsible for colluding with local miscellaneous troops and bandits. On the Korean army side, the defenses were also very carefully deployed. On the 8th and 9th, the fighting west of the Putongzhan ordinary station in Zihedian became more intense, with artillery exchanges. The Korean army's front line of defense extended north to Da Wang Bridge, south to the southwest of Putongzhan ordinary station, with Zihedian in the middle, which was the focus of the fighting between the two armies. Zihedian is located 20 li east of Xindian, Putongzhan ordinary station is 14 li southeast of Zihedian, and Da Wang Bridge is 30 li north of Zihedian. The mountain peaks rise and fall, and the terrain is precipitous, making it a natural battlefield. It is not easy for the Jin army to advance eastward. In order to resist the Korean army's offensive, Yan Xishan specially dispatched Zhongshan No. 3 armored train to assist in the battle. The armored train arrived in Jinan from Cangzhou early on the 9th and was immediately transferred to Xindian Station on the Jiaoji Railway. Mines were also planted near Xindian west of Zihedian. At present, residents near Zihedian are fleeing to various places.

At 6:00 PM on the 5th, the special service regiment of the Jin army Shi Fengming's force, Cui Jiantang's force, also made contact with the Korean army 30 li southeast of Zhangdian. Its 2nd Regiment Feng Daming's force opened fire with the Korean army south of Zihedian. The rest of the 4th Regiment Guo Ziming's force moved out in Boshan. The 1st Regiment Li Ganqing's force plotted to disturb Linzi. The guard regiment

Cai Guanjun's force plotted to disturb Qingzhou. The 2nd Regiment Wang Shaozhou's force plotted to disturb Zhuyezhen. The separate detachment Su Zhenhua's force plotted to disturb Guangrao. Since the Jin and Korean armies began contact on the evening of the 5th, the railway between Jinlingzhen and Xindian on the Jiaoji Railway was destroyed, and traffic between Qingdao and Jinan was interrupted. According to reliable information from the transportation sector, a section of the railway track between Jinlingzhen and Xindian had its screws removed by the military, and the rails were still floating on top and had not been moved. Therefore, the 6th train leaving from Jidong on the Jiaoji Railway on the 6th arrived at Zhangdian and was changed to the 5th train at 9:00 PM and returned to Jinan. On the same day, the 5th train leaving from Qingdao west arrived at Da Xu River and was changed to the 6th train and returned to Qingdao. The interruption of traffic on the Jiaoji Railway has caused diplomatic problems. There are rumors of protests and troop dispatches by the Japanese. At 9:30 AM on the morning of the 7th, Mr. Kagayama, the Japanese chief of the Jiaoji Railway Transportation Office, and Mr. Liang Shangdong, the newly appointed director of the administration, traveled from Jinan by special train to Zhangdian to meet with Zhang Yinwu to discuss solutions for restoring traffic. Kagayama will also travel from Zhangdian to Weixian to negotiate with Han Fuju. It is expected that the traffic between Qingdao and Jinan may still be restored. At 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 8th, the consuls of the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, and Japan held a meeting at the Japanese Consulate in Jinan to discuss ways to maintain traffic on the Jiaoji Railway, with both sides ceasing fire when passenger trains passed through the war zone, and resuming fire after the trains had passed. The text of the telegram is as follows: (The Jiaoji Railway is the communication line between Jinan and Qingdao and a major artery for transportation and communication. From the perspective of international transportation, it is indispensable for even one day. Please have Commissioner Sa (Fukkyun) on one side and Director Liang (Shangdong) on the other

to negotiate with the military authorities to ensure that both sides cease fire when passenger trains pass through in order to maintain traffic.) (9th)

Chen Jitang's Report After Returning to Guangdong 52

Chen Mingshu Criticizes the Reasons for Zhang Guijun's Defeat

A moment of silence at the Memorial Week to mourn Zhang Shide

Guangzhou dispatch: Yesterday (the 7th), military, political, and party circles held a joint memorial week at the Guangdong Provincial Party Headquarters Auditorium. After Chairman Chen Jitang performed the ceremonial rituals, Chen Jitang reported, stating that he had returned to the province from the front on the 4th. Regarding the recent fighting with Zhang Guijun in southern Hunan, it can be said that the enemy has been completely annihilated. Today, I can briefly report on the course of events. First, regarding party affairs and politics, the Central Committee held a Supervisory Committee meeting on June 19 and resolved various regulations, and the Guangdong provincial and municipal party committees will be re-elected. The Fourth Representative Congress of the entire province is about to be convened, and the organizational regulations of the congress are being drafted. Regarding the political aspect, the government is vigorously building Zhongshan Port and is scheduled to hold the port opening ceremony on July 20. Secondly, great progress has been made in completing highways and promoting good governance in various counties. Regarding the central military, our army on the Longhai Road has advanced towards Kaifeng, killing tens of thousands of enemies. The enemy on the Pinghan Line has lost contact. The Central Army's abandonment of Jinan on the Jinpu Line was a temporary strategic measure. Speaking of the Battle of Hengyang in Hunan Province, Zhang Guijun's forces and the remnants of Zhou Lan and Tang Shengming can be said to have been completely annihilated. After Zhang rebelled and disturbed Changsha, the three divisions of Jiang, Cai, and Li had already captured Hengzhou, Hengshan, and Hengyang. The Guilin rebel forces of Huang Shaohong and Gong Xuchu were still lingering around Qiyang and attacked our positions, but were repelled by Jiang's division. Commander Jiang decided to hold the east bank of Hengyang firmly. The rear forces, Yu's division and Huang's teaching brigade, were on alert in Yuechang Jiufeng. After the enemy retreated to Changsha, they invaded Leiyang via Youxian and Anren, and joined forces with Huang's rebel forces in Qiyang. On the 26th of last month, they attacked our troops stationed on the east bank of Hengyang. There were also casualties on our side in this battle. On the 27th, there was fierce fighting on the west bank. On the 28th, He Jian's 4th Route Army arrived in Hengzhou to take over the defense. On the 30th, Jiang and Li's two divisions launched a general offensive against the enemy, with Cai's division serving as a reserve force and Yang Tenghui fighting fiercely in close combat, hand-to-hand. On July 1, Shen Guanghan's brigade rushed to the front line, and the enemy collapsed completely, retreating straight to Qiyang. In this battle, the enemy suffered no less than 12,000 casualties. Many were captured by Hua Zhenzhong's brigade during the rout. It is a pity that our Brigade Commander Zhang Shide died in action due to being hit by a stray bullet while leading his troops. Now, in addition to sending teams to pursue the remaining enemies, Yu's division has been ordered to return to Guizhou to completely eliminate the remnants, etc.

Next, Chen Mingshu spoke, "Commander Chen has just reported, and I think everyone heard it with great satisfaction. Now, I will briefly supplement the reasons why Zhang Guijun was resolved this time, so that the public can understand. When the enemy attempted to enter Hunan, they could invade Wuhan. The Eighth Route Army was ordered to pursue, and at that time, they were no less than ten days away from the enemy, so they had to hurry into Hunan. After the division arrived in Anren, the enemy had already occupied Changsha. After our army captured Hengzhou, we heard that the enemy had returned to fight the Eighth Route Army. At that time, we thought that the enemy had seen the main force in Wuhan coming straight down, so they had to return. According to our initial expectations, Zhang Guijun would not be so bold. Later, they actually crossed Liling and Pingxiang and pressured our positions, which was really inexplicable. The enemy had no less than 20,000 men, and we already knew their combat effectiveness. Therefore, we discussed with Commander Chen and thought that we could order the three divisions of Jiang, Cai, and Li to go straight down, and the rear forces of Yu, Huang, etc. could join in, which would have a pincer effect and would be a legitimate military tactic. Later, we feared that the enemy would attack us in full force and would definitely fight desperately, and we were afraid that the rear forces would not arrive on time, so we did not do it. Therefore, we had to take surprise tactics. The three divisions of Jiang, Cai, and Li were all concentrated in Hengzhou, while the rear forces were in Yuechang. The enemy rushed forward and cut off Leiyang, but unexpectedly, they found nothing after arriving in Leiyang. At that time, Bai Chongxi did not know how to respond and was at a loss, so he attacked Jiang, Cai, and Li in Hengzhou again. On the 28th, there was a fierce battle around Qitang and Batang. On the 29th, Brigade Commander Zhang Shide fought with Yang Tenghui, and the enemy collapsed completely. Regarding this battle, I can say that the enemy has committed a major taboo in military strategy. After retreating to Changsha, they attacked Leiyang, and after arriving in Leiyang, they returned to Hengzhou. Being transferred east and west like this, they were exhausted. How could they withstand it? Therefore, the enemy suffered no less than 10,000 casualties this time. The result of their failure is here. Now they are fleeing back to their old nest in Guangxi. It is a pity that Brigade Commander Zhang Shide of the Ninth Brigade led his troops in the battle this time, resulting in his death on the battlefield, which is deeply regrettable. Now, please stand up and observe a moment of silence for Brigade Commander Zhang," etc.

Zhang Shide, commander of the 9th Brigade of the 61st Division, was killed by a bullet to the head in the Battle of Paishan in Hengyang one day. Commander Chen was deeply saddened upon hearing the news. He immediately ordered the business office to allocate 10,000 yuan for Zhang's memorial service and appointed Zhuang Weigang, director of the rear of the 61st Division, to prepare for the memorial service together with Chen Fuyuan, director of the rear of the 9th Brigade, and ordered all officers and soldiers in the rear to wear black armbands for three days to express their condolences. All affairs of the Ninth Brigade are temporarily handled by Division Commander Jiang Guangnai. It is said that the position of brigade commander will be filled by Zhang Yan, the regimental commander of the brigade. Zhang Yan is Zhang Shide's cousin.

Shantou Banks to be Banned 53

Due to excessive issuance of banknotes, destabilizing the financial system.

Shantou dispatch: Shantou banks and money changers have issued banknotes totaling as much as 5 million. In recent years, due to the decline in land prices, some have gone bankrupt and cannot redeem their notes. Therefore, last year, when Chen Guoqu was mayor, the city government submitted six proposed measures to the Department of Finance to be banned, stipulating that the city government, the central branch, and the chamber of commerce should jointly organize a review agency to implement the ban. However, over the past year, the city government has repeatedly convened meetings to organize a review agency, but the chamber of commerce has repeatedly used excuses to refuse to send representatives to attend, which has prevented the agency from being established. Recently, due to the gold price issue, silver merchants have resumed speculative business, which unfortunately failed, and the banks went bankrupt immediately, which has greatly affected the city's financial situation. The Department of Finance specially ordered the city government a few days ago to quickly comply with the measures and implement the ban. If the chamber of commerce still refuses to send representatives to form a review agency, then the city government will handle it together with the Central Bank. The reporter went to the city government yesterday to inquire about the progress of the ban from Mr. Ye Weiqing, director of the Finance Bureau, who said that a meeting is now scheduled for 2:00 PM on the 10th to organize a review agency. The six proposed measures are as follows: (1) The issuance of banknotes by various banks in Shantou City should be reviewed by an agency jointly organized by the city government, the central branch, and the chamber of commerce. First, the number of banknotes issued by each bank and the types and values of guaranteed real estate should be thoroughly and accurately investigated. Their valuations should be estimated separately and should not exceed 70 percent of the value. That is, real estate worth 10,000 yuan can only guarantee a value of 7,000 yuan. The method of valuation should be based on the general market situation. The amount of rent that can be obtained for every 10,000 yuan of property should be used as the standard for estimating the current rent of the real estate. In addition to real estate, a cash deposit of 20 percent should also be paid. That is, a bank issuing 10,000 yuan of banknotes should pay a cash deposit of 2,000 yuan. The remaining 8,000 yuan is allowed to be guaranteed by real estate. The guaranteed cash and real estate deeds are all kept by the review agency. (2) The issuance of banknotes by banks in Chaozhou and Meizhou prefectures should be handled in accordance with these measures. The city and county magistrates of each prefecture and city should jointly organize a review agency with the local chamber of commerce. (3) The banknotes issued in Shantou City and Chaozhou and Meizhou prefectures should be limited to the current amount and should not be issued excessively privately. Violators will be severely investigated. Those that have already been issued must be restricted to a maximum amount, and a plan for gradual reduction should be scheduled and recovered within a reasonable period. How to limit the amount and how to determine the time limit should be reviewed by the review agency based on the local situation and reported for approval. When contracting, the review agency should review the extent to which the contraction has been made, and the guaranteed real estate should be returned in proportion to the extent of the contraction. If it is impossible to contract, the guaranteed real estate will be auctioned off for compensation. The auction procedures are still handled by the chamber of commerce as before. (4) If the guarantees for the issuance of banknotes by various banks in Shantou City are not deemed adequate after review, they must be ordered to contract. Banks in Chaozhou and Meizhou prefectures must also be ordered to provide guarantees, otherwise they must be banned to maintain the financial system. (5) Banks that enjoy the benefits of issuing banknotes should be subject to taxes levied by the government. The standard for taxation should be 300 yuan per year for every 10,000 yuan of banknotes issued. Before the current issuance system is temporarily unified, the number of banknotes issued by each bank should be reported to the review agency for detailed registration in order to be totaled. (6) The face value of each banknote issued by a bank should not be less than 10 yuan.

(July 8th)

Harbin Market Fire 54

Over 500 buildings were destroyed.

Total losses exceeded one million yuan.

Harbin dispatch: On the morning of the 6th, the weather was overcast and rainy, and it cleared up in the afternoon, but the wind was very strong and did not stop until the evening. A fire broke out in the Jiangbin Market in Harbin City amidst this strong wind, destroying over 300 buildings and over 150 single-story houses. Total losses exceeded one million. The market outside the old Jiangdi levee in Daowai, Harbin, has been opened for many years. The houses are densely packed, and the construction is very poor. No fire prevention ditches are installed in Taiping Road, so once a fire broke out, it spread and could not be extinguished. The fire zone was the northern zone of the market. First, a three-story building near Changchun San Dao Street with 166 rooms was burned. The tenants downstairs were prostitutes, and the second and third floors were rented to small hotels, including Yuanfa Inn, Tianbao Inn, and Tongxin Inn. They owed months of rent, and the landlord Zou Xi repeatedly urged them to pay, but they refused. Recently, Zou sued the Binjiang County Government, which ruled that the tenants be evicted and the houses sealed. On the 5th of this month, the county magistrate sent personnel to execute the order. The three small hotel owners suddenly lost their jobs and resented the landlord. At 9:00 PM on the 6th of this month, they sneaked into an empty room in Yuanfa Inn and set fire to cotton soaked in kerosene. Because the room was unoccupied, it was not immediately noticed. At 9:15 PM, the flames were visible through the windows, and people nearby noticed and immediately reported to the police at the street corner. At that time, the market was crowded with people. Upon hearing the fire alarm, the order was disrupted, and men, women, old, and young ran to avoid it, blocking the road. By the time the fire trucks arrived, the road was already impassable. It took a long time to reach the vicinity of the fire scene. At that time, the fire had already engulfed the entire building due to the wind, and it spread to the neighboring houses. The fire brigade tried its best to put out the fire, but there were no wells nearby, making it difficult to get water, and the buildings were too high, making it difficult to fight the fire. They only inspected the nearby single-story houses for rescue. At 9:30 PM, the fire intensified, and six surrounding buildings and four single-story houses were all affected. The fire brigades of all public and private organizations in the city arrived one after another around 10:00 PM, but they were unable to put out the fire and allowed it to burn until 3:00 AM on the morning of the 7th. The entire area of over 340 buildings, over 150 single-story houses, and 60 sheds was reduced to ashes. After the incident, it was investigated that the burned landlords included Zou Xi, with 166 buildings and 87 single-story houses, Sun Ruyuan, with 132 buildings and 15 single-story houses, and Wang Jintang, with 44 buildings and 48 single-story houses. Among the burned businesses, those with larger capital and losses exceeding 20,000 yuan included Hengchang Lumber Company and Deshengchang Lumber Factory. The remaining 16 small hotels, 26 prostitutes, and 68 small businesses were statistically counted. Because the fire started around 9:00 PM, when it was still sultry and people had not yet gone to sleep, there were no deaths. It is said that all the landlords were insured, and the only ones suffering were the general small businesses. (7th)

Fierce Battle Between Zhejiang Naval Police and Pirates 55

Xiangshan Port Declares Martial Law

Zhejiang Province's coastal defense arrangements have always been very strict, so the various pirate gangs, though extremely fierce, have ultimately failed to succeed. Currently, with bandit gangs rampant in the inland counties of eastern Zhejiang, pirates are also seizing the opportunity to stir up trouble. Wang Wenhan, commander of the bandit suppression in the four prefectures of Ningbo, Shaoxing, Wenzhou, and Taizhou, and concurrently director of the Zhejiang Outer Seas Naval Police Bureau, recently received repeated secret reports that the Xin'ao and Sheng'ao pirate gangs have re-emerged and are plotting to disturb the peace on the seas. He immediately dispatched two teams of naval police and one squadron of guerilla troops, along with patrol ships, to patrol day and night. They encountered a group of about 500 pirates in the Qingzi Port area, and a fierce battle ensued, lasting about three hours. The pirates, unable to withstand the attack, dispersed in three directions. One group headed towards Xiangshan Port, one retreated directly to Shenjiamen Port, and the remaining group fled towards the North Yushan area. As a result, the Xiangshan County government, in order to prevent the spread of disaster, declared martial law. County Magistrate Zhang Zhouwen and the stationed security team and public security bureau discussed measures to implement strict inspections. At the same time, a telegram was sent to the Ministry of the Navy requesting the dispatch of warships for joint defense. It is now known that the Jingxing gunboat dispatched by the Ministry of the Navy, seeing that Xiangshan already had security measures in place, went directly to the Shenjiamen sea area to join the army and police in encircling and suppressing the pirates. The provincial government also dispatched an additional regiment of security troops yesterday to assist in the suppression. However, according to other news from fishermen and merchants, the Zhejiang naval police have already killed a pirate leader, and the remaining pirates have dispersed and gone into hiding. (14th)

Hangzhou Quick Notes 56

The provincial government received an order from the Ministry of Communications to investigate the two cases of collisions between the Wenfu and Quandali steamships operating in Wenzhou and Fuquan. The ministry has dispatched personnel to Zhejiang to conduct on-site investigations in Wenzhou together with personnel dispatched by the provincial government, to determine how to compensate and provide relief to the dozens of victims in Zhejiang. At the same time, the Yongjia County Magistrate and the Fourth District Navigation Administration Bureau have been ordered to report the findings of their investigations for review.

The Zhejiang Relief Association's procurement of unpolished rice to assist various counties in stabilizing rice prices is nearing completion. The association has approved 7,000 bags of rice for the four townships of Hang County. The remaining rice is less than 6,000 dan, and many counties still have a shortage of rice. The distribution will only be carried out to the extent possible.

Zhang Jun, the magistrate of Tiantai County, has been repeatedly accused of corruption and dereliction of duty. The Department of Civil Affairs has dispatched personnel to conduct a thorough investigation. Ye Wen, the magistrate of Changshan County, has monopolized the entire county's slaughter tax, which has been met with strong opposition from meat merchants. The Department of Finance and the Department of Civil Affairs have reportedly issued orders to the county to report the matter for review and handling.

The Department of Construction believes that the accounting personnel of its subordinate agencies are not competent enough due to a lack of specialized talent. Therefore, a specialized accounting personnel office has been established in the department. The accounting personnel of each agency will be directly appointed by the department, so that their knowledge and experience can be used to their full potential. In addition, accounting supervisors from the department will be dispatched to provide guidance and inspection at any time.

The Hangzhou municipal rice price stabilization factory is divided into five locations. It opened on May 1st, and this term has been specially extended for one month until the end of August. Shen, the general manager of the Three Warehouses, has already prepared sufficient rice for sale. However, the amount of rice sold daily at each factory has been slightly restricted to 25 dan to avoid financial strain. It is also known that the rice price stabilization bureau in the Guobao district attached to the city began on June 1st. The funds were raised locally, and the rice was purchased from the Three Warehouses at a fixed price. The end date is also the end of August.

The Hangzhou municipal residence and store property tax, since it was changed to a minimum of two yuan, has been difficult to collect due to the large population. There are places where those who are urged to pay simply ignore the request. The Finance Bureau of the municipal government has specially set the tax collection period to two months to expedite the collection of overdue taxes and replenish public funds.

Songjiang 57

Confession of Ye Xie Capture of Thieves: The county government recently received a secret report that Chen Adi, a bandit, and his bandit wife Chen Luo (the wife of Chen Xiuming, who was killed by his accomplices last year) are hiding in Xiaobazi Bridge, Eleventh District, Ye Xie, and are plotting to cause trouble in Punan. Magistrate Jin immediately secretly ordered Dong Futang, the chief of legal police, Inspector Zong, and Yuan, the squad leader of the second squad of the police team stationed in Ye, to go and arrest them together. Dong went to Ye on the 13th and, in the evening, went to the address to arrest them with the police team leader. Chen Adi was arrested first, and the bandit wife Chen Luo jumped onto the roof to escape, hiding in the sloping ditch of the roof. After being illuminated by electric torches, she was ordered to come down and was captured. Ruan Ashu, Chen Shigen, Chen Husheng, and others who lived with them were also taken to the county because they were suspected of involvement. They arrived in Songjiang on the afternoon of the 14th and were immediately interrogated by Judge Du. According to Chen Adi's confession, he did participate in the robbery of Yu Mingqing's house last winter and received three dou of white rice and trousers after the robbery. He also identified Chen Luo as having received three dou of white rice and a leather vest in the case. He refused to admit to the Zhuanghang arson case and the Shengzi Temple looting case. Chen Luo's confession was cunning and evasive. The other three, Ruan Ashu, Chen Shigen, and Chen Hu, all claimed to be living together and had nothing to do with the robbery. After the interrogation, they were ordered to be detained for review.

It was reported that the meeting resulted in the county magistrate being appointed as the director of the rural clearing bureau, with the chief of the public security bureau as the deputy director. Branch bureaus will be established in each district, with the district chief serving as the director of the branch bureau. The selection of a director and staff members to work in the bureau, as well as the planning of funds, will be discussed at the next preparation meeting.

Garrison Troops Seize a Pedestrian Carrying Corrosive Liquid in Shihudang: The garrison troops stationed at Shihudang yesterday seized Ji Erbao, a resident of Nanxun, Huzhou, who was carrying half a bottle of corrosive liquid. He was handed over to the county for interrogation. Judge Du interrogated him and learned that he had been a cook at the Shanghai Tongyun Company and that the corrosive liquid was left over from the company and he wanted to give it to a coppersmith shop next door. He had no other intentions. As a result, the court ordered him to be detained for review.

County Magistrate Huang issued instructions to the county education bureau to comply with the order.

When writing the draft, he was not fully conscious. He refused to reveal the reason, only shaking his head and weeping, saying that there were various reasons for his suicide.

After she entered the household, the couple was still harmonious. Unexpectedly, less than a year later, A'yu suddenly changed his behavior and spent his days wandering around. Despite his wife's kind劝劝, A'yu repeatedly refused to listen and often beat Chun'di. Recently, A'yu beat his wife severely for no reason, causing her to be covered in injuries. When Chun'di's birth mother, Jiang Li, learned about this, she submitted a report to the Public Security Bureau requesting that the police arrest A'yu and bring him to justice. After receiving the report, Huang Zhenbai, the director of the Public Security Bureau, immediately dispatched detectives and police officers to the countryside to make the arrest. Ministry of Education Prohibits the Transportation and Sale of Ancient Books 68

Our newspaper reported from Nanjing on the 14th that the Ministry of Education stipulates that all woodblock books published in our country more than fifty years ago, as well as [items such as Song Dynasty hall editions, etc., must be regarded as ancient books, properly preserved, and prohibited from transportation and sale.

The Financial Difficulties of Local Education in Jiangsu and Their Remedies

Document from the Education Department of Jiangsu Province to the Provincial Government 69

(Zhenjiang Correspondence) The Education Department of Jiangsu Province submits a document to the Provincial Government regarding the current dire situation of local education funding in the province and points to which attention should be paid when planning comprehensively for its allocation, for consideration. The original text reads:

“Finance is the mother of all administrations, and education is the foundation for a hundred years. In all planning, these two aspects should be given equal consideration. In particular, the education sector should only advance and not regress. Therefore, it is essential that education funding be continuously increased and not reduced in order to safeguard its stability, especially by implementing (independent education funding). For this reason, the texts of (increasing education funding and ensuring its independence) are considered key principles of the Party's political program. Now, at the beginning of political tutelage, vigorously promoting universal education should be the basic work for training the masses and promoting autonomy. Therefore, increasing education funding and ensuring its independence should be prioritized and thoroughly implemented as important policies. In order to carry out this policy, the Finance Department, recognizing the disorder in various county affairs, proposed a plan to reform land taxes and county finances, intending to start with investigation and statistics, and to redistribute all surtax revenue according to percentage ratios. This has been approved by the Provincial Government's 307th Committee meeting. This is a fundamental and necessary measure to reform accounting and administration. The current dire situation of local education funding in this province and the points to which attention should be paid when planning comprehensively are already known to the Provincial Government, and no further elaboration is needed to maintain regulation and harmonization. However, due to my responsibility, I cannot remain silent. I hereby analyze and present them for consideration.

The amount of funding should depend on the degree of need. Speaking only in terms of quantity, the proportion of education funding to other county expenditures may seem slightly high. However, considering the needs of the education sector, many necessary facilities have not been established, and many necessary programs have not been implemented in as much as 80% or 90% of counties. This phenomenon of supply failing to meet demand is not a fabrication of the Education Department. For example, in terms of free education, according to the statistics of the 17th year of the Republic (1928), the proportion of school-age children enrolled in school in each county is generally between 15% and 20%. In the counties with the fewest enrolled children, the proportion is only 4%. Thus, the majority of school-age children in each county are unable to attend school due to the failure to extend free education year by year, thus losing their foundation as sound citizens. What could be more painful than this? As for social education, it is still in its infancy, with everything needing to be done, so there is no need to elaborate. In our country, where the number of illiterates accounts for 80% of the population, the low level of culture is alarming. The only way to improve it is to gradually implement free and social education. The National Education Conference this year resolved to complete the plan of free education in 20 years and social education in 6 years, which is a wise decision. Therefore, the implementation of free and social education is not enough to meet the minimum needs. The situation of other general education is similar. Therefore, the education funding in each county is actually at the minimum level when measured against its needs. Moreover, summing up the existing sources of county education funding, such as busy grain transport surtax, busy grain transport with general levy, universal mu donation, and education mu donation, most of it comes from farmland. In recent years, due to banditry, natural disasters, and poor autumn harvests, the actual revenue received is far from the fixed amount. The original plan for free education mu donation was to increase it to 1 jiao 6 fen per mu, but now each county generally collects 8 fen, and some collect only 4 fen. The method of increasing it year by year has been difficult to implement. Thus, the fixed education funding, which is already at the minimum level, has become like the sheep announced but not provided for sacrifice. Since the establishment of the Education Department last year, the financial difficulties of county education funding have been almost constant. Salary demands are frequently heard, and education strikes occur repeatedly. Even today, under the system of independent education funding, where the foundation is relatively solid and changes are more difficult, the current situation is already so difficult. If the system were changed, the disputes would inevitably worsen, and the Finance Department may not achieve the effect of reforming finance, while education would already be bankrupt. This is why the Education Department dares not help but express its concerns. After repeated consideration, regarding the measures to reorganize finance, there seem to be several matters that should be decided in advance, to ensure that they do not contradict the Finance Department's proposals and that the current state of education can be temporarily maintained. I respectfully list them below:

First, no matter what percentage of the total county expenditure education funding constitutes, the original amount of funding in each county must be maintained as the minimum. It is well known that the majority of local education is elementary school, and the work of elementary school teachers is arduous and their salaries are meager. The Education Department, after reviewing the current situation, is angered and worried about it, but is unable to improve it due to financial constraints. I am powerless and full of sighs. I had no choice but to formulate a standard for the distribution of elementary school education funding, the main purpose of which is that the source of education funding is not easy to obtain and should be used economically and efficiently. At the same time, it is also intended to eliminate unnecessary expenses and stabilize salaries, so that elementary school teachers can make a stable living within this minimum limit, so as to be better than the past, when salaries were owed for months and teachers were constantly complaining. Since the Education Department formulated this standard for elementary school funding, all extravagant expenses have been eliminated and cannot be reduced any further. If the total county education funding is suddenly reduced at this time, there will be no extravagant expenses to cut and no surplus funds to supplement. It will be necessary to suspend some of the existing schools at all levels and social education institutions in order to balance the revenue and expenses. This will not only cause panic in the education sector of the entire province, but will also cause the small number of children who are already in school to lose their education and the majority of teachers who have jobs to suddenly become unemployed. The consequences are something that the Education Department cannot bear to say. This is the first point that should be noted.

Second, the education budget should still be prepared separately and should not be mixed with other local budgets. The provincial education funding of Jiangsu Province has been independently managed since five or six years ago. The separate preparation of county education funding budgets has also been approved by the Provincial Government and ordered to be followed. All these existing elements of independent education funding should be preserved. This is to fulfill the political program from above and to comply with the fixed decision from below. Now that the education budgets of each county for the 18th year of the Republic (1929) have been prepared in accordance with the order, the 19th year can be handled according to the previous case, which is a logical and easy way to proceed. It seems that the preparation of the entire county budget can also achieve a mutually beneficial effect. This is the second point that should be noted.

Third, education funding should be stored separately and should not be arbitrarily misappropriated by the county magistrate or finance director to prevent embezzlement. There are already special chapters for the safekeeping of education mu donations, with strict restrictions. However, the collecting agencies in various counties blatantly disregard them and arbitrarily misappropriate large amounts of mu donations and other education taxes. Such cases are still frequently seen and cannot be listed one by one. Whether it is for public or private reasons, once discovered, there is no way to investigate. Some are ordered to strictly pursue the embezzled funds, and some are ordered to be repaid by the successors. Even if the embezzled funds are recovered and repaid, the education funding has already suffered from the disorder. Recently, the Education Department has sent no fewer than several cases to the Finance Department requesting measures to recover the embezzled funds, which is clear evidence. If, in the future, all special education funds are included in the overall allocation, the restrictions will be lifted, and the misappropriation will be even more convenient. To prevent repeating past mistakes, it is necessary to strictly define the boundaries and continue to use the special fund method for separate safekeeping as a guarantee. This is the third point that should be noted.

Fourth, the original accumulated education funds in each county should still be stored in special accounts and should not be used on the pretext of emergency. The funding crisis and hardship of education have been completely described without reservation. However, some general observers may still think that the education budget includes methods for extracting funds and first and second reserve funds, and each county must follow the prescribed proportion for extraction. Therefore, although education funding is tight, there is still a surplus for future planning, which is not as bad as it is said. However, the fund item is used to adapt to the needs of the education sector and expand it year by year, and is also as indispensable as fees for ceremonies. As for the reserve fund rate, it is used to offset the reduction in autumn assessment to avoid the malpractice of virtual revenue and actual expenditure in the budget. In fact, there is no actual revenue. However, I am afraid that as soon as the order for overall allocation is issued, those who do not know the situation will be dazzled by the names of funds and reserve funds, and will rush to divide up the funds for immediate gratification. Those that are not actually received can be left aside. However, if the remaining education funds are all donated to this area, it will not help other administrative income much, but it will be extremely harmful to the future of education. I am extremely concerned about this and believe it is not possible. This is the fourth point that should be noted.

The above four points are all essential issues for maintaining local education in Jiangsu. They are based on common principles and the actual needs to stabilize the current state of education while striving to reorganize finance in order to uphold the purpose of the Provincial Government in attaching importance to the basic work of political tutelage. Therefore, I dare not avoid being tedious and state the facts directly. Whether they are appropriate or not, I respectfully await your review and decision and prompt implementation for the public good. Respectfully submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee, Chen Xian, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Department.

Shanghai Jiangnan Boy Scouts Arrive in Kobe 72

A warm welcome for Sino-Japanese friendship

(Kobe News) The Shanghai Jiangnan University Boy Scout delegation of 42 members, who visited Japan for inspection, arrived safely at 2:30 PM on July 11th aboard the Nagasaki Maru. Representatives of the Japan Boy Scout League and the Chinese and Japanese students from the two schools lined up at the pier to welcome them. County and city authorities also sent personnel to greet them. After exchanging greetings, the Overseas Chinese Boy Scout representatives, Zeng Guangke, Chen Genlin, and Li Wanzhi, led them to visit the Chinese Consulate General in Kobe, the Hyogo Prefectural Office, the Kobe City Hall, various Japanese newspapers, and the Kuomintang branch. After a short rest, they went to the Maru Restaurant to attend the welcome dinner hosted by the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce. Chinese and Japanese boy scouts shared stories and talked cordially, expressing their friendship. That night, they took a train to Osaka, where they were hosted by the All Japan Boy Scout League for one night. Then, they traveled to Nara, Kyoto, and other famous scenic spots for sightseeing. Initially, the representatives of the Kobe Overseas Chinese Boy Scouts had contacted the Japanese authorities to arrange for them to visit the Kawasaki Shipyard and the Kawanisi Airfield. However, due to a telegram from the Japanese Boy Scout League with other preparations, the order was changed. A grand welcome will be held again when the Shanghai University Boy Scouts return to Kobe from Tokyo, it is said.

The Start of Summer School in Shanghai 75

The summer school run by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau held its opening ceremony at Jingye Middle School on Jukui Street yesterday morning. Director Chen, Mayor’s representative Cen Dezhang, Jiang Wenyu, and about 400 attendees were present. Director Chen chaired the meeting and conducted the ceremony.

The chairman delivered a speech, stating that since Shanghai became a municipality, there have been two summer training sessions and training institutes. This year, according to the resolution of the National Education Conference, provinces and municipalities can set up summer schools, and counties and cities under the provinces can set up summer training sessions. Therefore, the name of this session is determined to be the first Shanghai Municipal Summer School, and the period of in-service training is set at five or seven years. During this period, elementary school teachers and teachers who have passed the certification must continuously attend the previous summer school. Graduates of normal schools, higher normal schools, and university normal departments must also continuously attend two summer schools. The summer school is run by the education administrative agency, and the attendees are elementary school teachers, directly seeking in-service training for teachers and indirectly thinking about all students. Without good teachers, there will be no good students, and without students, there will be no citizens in the future. Therefore, we attach importance to this summer school, so that teachers can take this opportunity to acquire some new knowledge, skills, and methods, and then use new methods, skills, and knowledge to instill in the students. Recently, there has been a misconception that teachers have to come to summer school in order to teach. Because of this misconception, there is a phenomenon of asking for leave on the pretext of illness, which is a big mistake. I think that teachers should rush to join the summer school as soon as they hear about it, because this is an opportunity for teachers to improve themselves, and it is not related to others. This year, there are several special courses with several special lecturers. Education, whether it is skills, methods, or knowledge, is advancing with each passing day. Summer schools can provide everyone with new and advanced information from the mouths of various lecturers. In the past, some elementary school teachers have had erroneous thoughts and reactionary behaviors. We hope that during this period, everyone will encourage and supervise each other, gain improvement and understanding, and pay attention to moral cultivation. The responsibility of teachers is very great. If the students taught in the future commit crimes, it is the teacher's fault. Finally, we should thank the lecturers for taking on the lectures in the hot summer, and the officials and guests who participated in the opening ceremony today.

The mayor's speech was delivered by Cen Dezhang, who said that some people think that they have reached a considerable level, so why bother to attend summer school again? This is a mistake. Education is to enable us to adapt to the environment and increase our ability. The environment is constantly changing, and so is education. Elementary school teachers are usually busy with their homework and have no time for sufficient research. Summer school provides you with an opportunity to research. The establishment of summer schools by the education administrative authorities is a contribution to you, not just for teachers to participate in. In the past, a scholar who was the head of a school would always go to the teachers' offices during his spare time to see if the books on their desks were often changed and beneficial. Otherwise, at the end of the semester, he would not renew their contracts because they did not seek to improve themselves at any time. There is no end to learning. Teachers must move forward without end.

Lecturer's speech (1) Fang Bingguan said that human evolution is based on the fact that society is constantly changing. If they advance and I do not, I will become outdated. Regarding the phonetic symbols, the first time was for the national sound word inspection, and the second time was for the Beijing sound safe mother, but both were unsuccessful. The third time was for the national sound word origin in the second year of the Republic of China (1913), and in the seventh year (1918), the Ministry of Education officially publicized it, taking the Beijing sound as the standard. People in various places could not get used to it, and the emotions on society were not cured, so there was an improvement of the phonetic safe mother this year. The national sound alphabet of the past was to unify the pronunciation first and then popularize education. Now it is to unify the pronunciation in the popularization of education. The national sound problem has undergone several improvements. We cannot be outdated again. Pay attention to the symbols. There is no survey of the national sounds in various provinces at present. It is estimated that it will be completed by the end of the year at the latest. (2) Jiang Wenyu said that he had a little feeling about the summer school. There was no so-called summer vacation before the establishment of new-style education, only annual vacations or busy vacations in rural farming seasons. Now the school has summer vacations and summer schools, which seems contradictory. In fact, it is not contradictory. The private schools of the past were simple, but the schools of today are complicated. The administrative aspects should have finished and prepared future matters. The students should also have a considerable rest or work. Therefore, the summer vacation is not released for no reason, and it also provides teachers with an opportunity to supplement their knowledge and ability, especially elementary school teachers. Although they say that they teach, learn, and do at the same time, there is always more output than input, and new knowledge and skills are needed at all times. Therefore, the summer school is the most beneficial for elementary school teachers. There are many types of summer schools, but they are all to meet the needs, or for further education, or for studying something. Elementary school teachers are studying new methods and new theories to meet the needs. The second is to increase work efficiency. After receiving the training of the summer school and gaining new skills, the work efficiency will naturally increase. The third is to hope for occupational improvement. Occupation is a large part of life, and teachers are the foundation of the country. It is good to improve at all times. I hope that you will recognize the use of summer school, and I wish you occupational improvement.

Summer school staff: Principal Chen Dezheng, Director of the Education Department Tang Shouqian, Registry Zhang Yanggao, Ding Chongxuan, Lecture Department Wei Shinan, Chen Yu, General Affairs Department Director Fu Fuwenwen, Secretary Cheng Yuhou, General Affairs Peng Yan, Accountant Tang Puyu, Reception Zhou Shang, Training Director Jiang Hongqi, Dormitory Ge Mingjun, Training Chen Songchun, Activities Zhang Ruizhen, Zhong Shuyang

Athletes and Manuscript Writing 94

Tilden is dismissed from the tennis tournament for signing and writing newspaper manuscripts, which violates the competition rules

Athletes' compliance with the rules

According to a United London dispatch on the 7th, the American Tennis Association requested that Tilden, who won the 1930 All England singles championship, represent them at the European-American inter-regional finals held in Paris on the 18th, 19th, and 20th. However, Mr. Tilden refused the authorities' request because he had already signed a contract with a newspaper to write special reports on the inter-regional finals, which conflicted with the American Tennis Association's rule that a tennis player who has participated in a competition may not sign and send manuscripts to newspapers and magazines. However, this is only a problem for the European-American inter-regional competition. As for whether to attend the Chalenge tournament, it depends on Tilden's contract with the newspaper magazine. This can be decided as another problem.

To Laugh it Off, Haike 99

A: Every day when I return home, I tell my wife everything I experienced outside. Therefore, she is very satisfied and calls me a good husband.

B: Every day when I return home, I tell my wife everything I never experienced. She believes it without a doubt and is very satisfied, even calling me a model husband.

A: Do you like the joke I told?

B: It's good, but it's as old as my grandfather.

A: Your complexion is very rosy and your body is very strong. What is your secret to health?

B: Yes. Because I never ask doctors for advice or take medicine.

A: You are truly the number one idiot in the world.

B: I don't dare to accept such praise. Everything has to let you, my big brother, take the lead. How dare I presume to go first?

A drowning person (taking out a silver dollar from his pocket and giving it to the person who saved him): Thank you for saving my life today. This dollar is to pay for your labor.

Rescuer: You get what you pay for. For such a small matter, you've given me too much.

A charitable old lady (soliciting donations from a wealthy man): Sir, please do a good deed and donate a few dozen dollars.

Wealthy man: You've come to the wrong place. I don't have any money.

Charitable old lady: Then how much do you want? Please tell me. I've already raised some money elsewhere. This money was originally for the poor.

A Unique Wedding, Pillow Stone 100

A guest came from Beiping, and I asked him about things in the north. Are there any novelties recently? The guest said no. The guest was the director of the affiliated middle school of Fu Jen Catholic University in Beiping, so I asked again about the academic circles in the north. Are there any novelties? The guest said yes. He then described a marriage that could be used for conversation. (The following is what the guest said) A certain Mr. So-and-so, who teaches Party Ideology at our school, is from Hunan. He is also quite capable of fulfilling his duties in teaching methods and is full of new ideas. He often does things that are unexpected. His personality is also very humorous, so people like to associate with him. One day, he suddenly announced his wedding date and showed the address of the Huabei Grand Hotel. The guest, as a colleague, gave him a congratulatory couplet. On the scheduled day, the guest and the other guests arrived one after another. There were no banners or decorations in the hall. The two newlyweds were nowhere to be found. Some doubted and even said that he was attracting people by making excuses. Suddenly, Mr. So-and-so was seen leading his new wife by the hand, walking side by side and skipping happily. The so-called groom was still wearing his usual green woolen suit. The so-called bride was only wearing a black skirt, the standard clothing of women in academic circles. The man did not wear a flower on his lapel, and the woman did not wear a trailing veil. After bowing slightly to the crowd, they went on stage to give a speech. He said that their marriage was the newest style. No introducer was needed, and no officiant was needed, because their marriage came from free love. Why need an introducer? All the guests present know that they are married today, so what need is there for an officiant? Furthermore, they didn't change their usual clothes, and there were no temporary decorations. All the bothersome expenses were completely eliminated. Isn't this the newest style of marriage? Everyone laughed loudly and applauded. Some asked the bride to announce the story of their love. The bride spoke eloquently, saying: I am also from Hunan. I taught with him at a certain school in Hangzhou. We got along because of our compatible personalities. He loved me, and I loved him. We were very close. However, we never mentioned marriage. Soon after, he went to study in Tokyo. Another person tried to destroy our friendship. When he heard about it, he rushed back, eliminated the rival in love, and proposed to me. I agreed. However, it was not carried out. I returned to Hunan because my mother was ill, and when I went to Hangzhou again, he had disappeared. A year passed. I happened to come here to find a job, and we reunited. Now I can fulfill the marriage contract here. This is the short history of our love. The crowd laughed again. Later, the groom's former teacher was invited to give a speech. He said that their wedding today was the newest style and could be used as a model for social weddings, but it was still too troublesome. If it were my youth

North American Myth, Heart Buddha 102

In areas where people's intelligence is closed, superstitious things appear in layers. If in civilized countries, the sayings of gods and ghosts are self-defeating. Only recently in Kansas City, America, KansasCity. Zheng Xuan Fu Mu Ma speaks, filling the city with wind and rain. This is also beyond the norm. In the early days, there was a harness company in Gansha City FosterHelnreichWagnerHarnssCo. A wooden horse stood in front of the door. When the company was booming, the horse seemed to represent the glorious era of horses. Da Shunqi every day. The company has been closed for many years.

Mr. J·J·Foste, General Manager of the Company, lives in retirement in his apartment on Weston Street. One. He happened to go to the small room on the roof of the building one day. The wooden horse stood there abruptly. He could not help but feel saddened. This once prominent wooden horse was abandoned in the pile of waste. He had not expected this at first. Life in old age is also like this. After a long time of sighing, Mr. Fu thought to himself: If the glorious era of this horse class is permanently stationed, how can the bright and splendid era of material civilization come? To comfort his grief. Therefore, he intends to give this ancient relic of historical value to Henry Ford, the creator of material civilization, so that it can be preserved in his Dearbern Museum. Ford agreed. Then he was transported to the hospital in a Ford truck as a souvenir of the transportation industry. When the wooden horse was transported onto the truck, the horse suddenly said to Mr. Fu. (Henry Ford made me fail. I should give me a place to live and hear that I will be sent to the museum, so I can rest easy from now on.) Mr. Fu was shocked. The incident gradually spread to nearby citizens and was shocked as a magic horse. News reporters from all over the world rushed to hear the news and regarded it as a rare piece of information. People in our country call things that have been around for a long time to become refined. This is what it means. The horse is gray and 16 hands high. The mane and tail are decorated with real horse hair. The skeleton is actually tied with paper, and the local citizens are accustomed to calling it Woodenhorse.

Eastern Journey Impressions (7) 104

(7) Osaka's Beauty Seat

From Kobe to Osaka, the train takes one hour. Osaka is one of Japan's six major cities. The six major cities are Tokyo, Osaka, Kyoto, Kobe, Nagoya, and Yokohama. Osaka is particularly the center of industry and commerce. Japan's largest industrial manufacturers and textile factories are concentrated here, making commerce very prosperous, first in Japan. The total population of the prefecture is 3,357,600, ranking second in the country and sixth in the world. Tokyo has the most, with 4,982,200 people (according to last year's report by the Japan Statistics Bureau). Osaka's streets are wide and clean, and the buildings are tall and magnificent. In the bustling city, there are many vehicles and pedestrians. When the reporter arrived in Osaka, it was almost dusk. Before long, ten thousand homes were illuminated with lights and electric lights, with red and green electric current advertisements everywhere. Transportation is even more convenient than in Shanghai, with trams running in all directions. For longer distances, one can take long-distance trams, which run every two minutes. Taxis can also be hired along the way. Within the city, regardless of distance, each ride costs one yen per day, so there are many taxis on the streets. It is very difficult for the police to maintain traffic. The congestion in front of the station is particularly severe, with a well-known police officer stationed there permanently, responsible for directing traffic. The officer's actions are almost frantic, gesticulating constantly, without a moment's rest. People stop when he signals them to stop, and proceed when he signals them to proceed, keeping order perfectly. Many people stop to watch. The reporter also stood for a few minutes, admiring his courage in performing his duties. Osaka and Tokyo are twelve hours apart by train. From April 1st of last year, Japan Air Transport Co., Ltd. started the Keihan Air Mail service, flying once every morning to carry passengers and mail, reaching the people in two hours, which is very convenient. The one-way fare is thirty yen, which is not much different from the first-class train fare, so business is very prosperous. Osaka has all kinds of entertainment venues, and the "Beauty Seat" is the most popular. The "Beauty Seat" is a variation of a coffee shop, with extremely beautiful young women as hostesses, providing tea, wine, and various other foods and drinks. Business hours are from 9:00 PM to 2:00 AM. The reporter visited once with Mr. Zeng Yanhua. Several male servants stand at the entrance, loudly inviting guests to enter, their duties similar to the turtle slaves in Shanghai. The interior is decorated elegantly and pleasantly, with bamboo frames covered with paper flowers and leaves, shaped realistically, and decorated with small green electric lights in between, making it even more luxurious. In the center, there is a small stage with scenery. At the corner of the stage, there is a radio broadcasting dance music, but you can't actually hold hands and dance. There are a dozen or so female hostesses, dressed gorgeously, with thick layers of face powder. They speak softly and gently. As soon as a guest arrives, they rush forward to sit beside them and provide attentive service, with warm and affectionate words that intoxicate people. The meal is mostly a few bottles of beer and a plate of broad beans, but the price is surprisingly high. Some linger for hours, unwilling to leave, because the drunkard's heart is not in the wine. Japanese women are extremely docile, treating their husbands like their second parents, never daring to resist in the slightest. They consider drinking and sensual pursuits to be natural and dare not interfere. Therefore, the business of the "Beauty Seat" is becoming increasingly prosperous. After several visits, one becomes a regular customer. Then, if you use clothes and accessories to win their favor, it is very easy to win their hearts. Countless Japanese men are addicted to the "Beauty Seat," wasting time and losing their jobs, which is a great disaster. The "Beauty Seat" is a specialty of Osaka. Recently, some have started to open in Ginza, Tokyo. On the day of opening, the threshold was broken. It is expected that after a few months, the prosperity will not be less than that of Osaka. The "Beauty Seat" business in Japan is still in its infancy.

Or not, they consider themselves rare commodities.

In Saigon, French Indochina, there is a huge zoo with a rich collection of birds, beasts, and aquatic animals, especially many strange creatures. There is a turtle with a triangular shell. One corner at the front is the head, and the two corners at the bottom are the two hind legs. The rest is the same as ordinary turtles. There is also a creature that looks like a turtle and a beast, huge and unparalleled. From a distance, it looks like a car. On closer inspection, it has a shell on its back like a turtle, and its head and feet also have similar features. This is what my friend Mr. Wu saw in Saigon. He told me about it when he returned.

In my Changtianning Temple, there is a release pond where turtles are released. Hundreds of them live together. The monks feed them twice a day. When it is time to feed them, the turtles are hidden at the bottom of the water. You only need to clap your hands a few times, and the turtles will hear the sound and compete to come to the surface, raising their heads to look at people, with tens of thousands of heads trembling, creating a spectacular sight. The food given is bran, which is sprinkled on the surface of the water. They compete to eat it like the five-colored big fish in the Jade Spring of West Lake. After eating, they sink again and disappear in an instant. Those who visit the temple and want to see the turtles only need to clap their hands to see them. The turtles know to eat when they hear the sound. They are spiritual creatures. However, sometimes they are played by people, which seems like people's intelligence backfiring on them.

I heard that someone in Wumen named Jia had suffered a series of misfortunes. A geomancer told his family that the feng shui of his father's tomb was not good, which had caused this. So they chose a site to move the tomb. When the tomb was opened, they found that water was stored under the coffin like a basin. Two turtles, golden in color, were resting in the water, their heads and feet retracted, like mandarin ducks sleeping soundly. Jia said, "This is a turtle's geomancy. It will definitely bring me good fortune in the future, but now is not the time." He quickly put the coffin back and covered it, keeping it intact. Later, Jia became even more unfortunate. People said that the earth's energy had been泄露, so it did not work. This is all superstitious talk, which is laughable to hear. However, it is strange how the two turtles were hidden under the coffin and why they regarded it as a paradise.
